# Events to rename China/Chinese Imperial empires and to grant temple names to their rulers on death

# by Silverswee(e)per

# TODO: Possibly allow reconversion to old pagan religion with HF, if it is acceptable (not a priority right now)

namespace = nameofchina

##### Inheritance

### Inheritance of China within the same dynasty, no longer Chinese Imperial due to wrong religion

# Inform the new EoC, give them the option to convert, and remove all Grace if they don't
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.1
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_1
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_1
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = no
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_dlc = "Jade Dragon"
				has_dlc = "Rajas of India"
			}
			OR = {
				secret_religion = FROMFROM
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = chinese_group
						culture = khitan
						culture = tangut
						culture = jurchen
						culture = mongol
						culture = viet
						culture_group = koreanic
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
						religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
						religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
						religion = bon # Tibet
						religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = chinese_pagan
						religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
						#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
						religion = korean_pagan
						religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
						religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_1 # Convert to Taoist
		
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		
		religion = taoist
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOR = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = chinese_pagan
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
				NOR = {
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
					religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
					religion = bon # Tibet
					religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = chinese_pagan
					religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
					#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
					religion = korean_pagan
					religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
					religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					culture_group = chinese_group
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_1 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				secret_religion = taoist
			}
		}
		
		#log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		#log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		#log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.2 }
		}
		
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.2
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_2
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_2
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_2 # I see...
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}



### Inheritance of China within the same dynasty, suddenly Chinese Imperial

# Inform the new EoC, let them pick a new name for China if China isn't named
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.3
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_3
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_3
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_tang_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = TANG
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Tang Empire"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.4 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				dynasty = 1051150 # Li
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_jin_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = JIN
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Jin Empire"
			adjective = "Jin"
			set_title_flag = jin_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.4 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				culture = jurchen
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = jin_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_wei_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = WEI
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Wei Empire"
			adjective = "Wei"
			set_title_flag = wei_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.4 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = wei_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3

				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5

			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_NAMEOFCHINA_3 # More options!
		set_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
		repeat_event = { id = nameofchina.3 }
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes

			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_qi_trigger = yes

			modifier = {

					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = yin_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_shun_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = SHUN
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Shun Empire"
			adjective = "Shun"

	}

# Inform the world - dynasty name kept

	id = nameofchina.6
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_6
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_6
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_6 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.7
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_7
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_7
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_7 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

			clr_title_flag = tang_china
			clr_title_flag = jin_china
			clr_title_flag = wei_china
			clr_title_flag = qi_china
			clr_title_flag = zhou_china
			clr_title_flag = han_china
			clr_title_flag = qin_china
			clr_title_flag = yan_china
			clr_title_flag = zhao_china
			clr_title_flag = liao_china
			clr_title_flag = yuan_china
			clr_title_flag = xia_china
			clr_title_flag = qing_china
			clr_title_flag = dai_china
			clr_title_flag = cheng_china
			clr_title_flag = liang_china
			clr_title_flag = song_china
			clr_title_flag = ming_china
			clr_title_flag = shu_china
			clr_title_flag = wu_china
			clr_title_flag = chu_china
			clr_title_flag = yue_china
			clr_title_flag = yin_china
			clr_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		#log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		#log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		#log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.12 }
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

	id = nameofchina.11
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_11
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_11
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_11 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.14
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_14
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_14
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_14 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}



### Usurpation/conquest of China by other dynasty, suddenly Chinese Imperial

# Inform the new EoC, let them pick a new name for China
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.15
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_15
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_15
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		clr_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhou_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = jin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wei_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		}
		if = {

			clr_title_flag = zhou_china

			clr_title_flag = qing_china

			clr_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Tang Empire"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = grace.999 } # Chinese princess (and Grace) update
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.16 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				dynasty = 1051150 # Li
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
		}

			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = grace.999 } # Chinese princess (and Grace) update
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.16 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = yin_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_shun_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = SHUN
		
		e_china = {
			clr_title_flag = tang_china
			clr_title_flag = jin_china
			clr_title_flag = wei_china
			clr_title_flag = qi_china
			clr_title_flag = zhou_china
			clr_title_flag = han_china
			clr_title_flag = qin_china
			clr_title_flag = yan_china
			clr_title_flag = zhao_china
			clr_title_flag = liao_china
			clr_title_flag = yuan_china
			clr_title_flag = xia_china
			clr_title_flag = qing_china
			clr_title_flag = dai_china
			clr_title_flag = cheng_china
			clr_title_flag = liang_china
			clr_title_flag = song_china
			clr_title_flag = ming_china
			clr_title_flag = shu_china
			clr_title_flag = wu_china
			clr_title_flag = chu_china
			clr_title_flag = yue_china
			clr_title_flag = yin_china
			clr_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Shun Empire"
			adjective = "Shun"
			set_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = grace.999 } # Chinese princess (and Grace) update
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.16 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					year = 1200
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = shun_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_NAMEOFCHINA_15 # More options!
		clr_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
		repeat_event = { id = nameofchina.15 }
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world - new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.16
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_16
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_16
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_16 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
}



### Usurpation/conquest of China by other dynasty, no longer Chinese Imperial due to wrong religion

# Inform the new EoC, give them the option to convert, and reset the name of China if they do not
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.17
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_17
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_17
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = no
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		clr_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhou_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		clr_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_tang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = jin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_jin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wei_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wei_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qi_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qi_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = han_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_han_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = zhao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_zhao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liao_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liao_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yuan_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yuan_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = xia_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_xia_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = qing_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_qing_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = dai_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_dai_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = cheng_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_cheng_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = liang_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_liang_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = song_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_song_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = ming_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_ming_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = wu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_wu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = chu_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_chu_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yue_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yue_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = yin_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_yin_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					has_title_flag = shun_china
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = formerly_shun_china
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_dlc = "Jade Dragon"
				has_dlc = "Rajas of India"
			}
			OR = {
				secret_religion = taoist
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = chinese_group
						culture = khitan
						culture = tangut
						culture = jurchen
						culture = mongol
						culture = viet
						culture_group = koreanic
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
						religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
						religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
						religion = bon # Tibet
						religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = chinese_pagan
						religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
						#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
						religion = korean_pagan
						religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
						religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_17 # Convert to Taoist
		
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		
		religion = taoist
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOR = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = chinese_pagan
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
				NOR = {
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
					religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
					religion = bon # Tibet
					religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = chinese_pagan
					religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
					#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
					religion = korean_pagan
					religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
					religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					culture_group = chinese_group
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
		}
		
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.19 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_17 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				secret_religion = taoist
			}
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			clr_title_flag = tang_china
			clr_title_flag = jin_china
			clr_title_flag = wei_china
			clr_title_flag = qi_china
			clr_title_flag = zhou_china
			clr_title_flag = han_china
			clr_title_flag = qin_china
			clr_title_flag = yan_china
			clr_title_flag = zhao_china
			clr_title_flag = liao_china
			clr_title_flag = yuan_china
			clr_title_flag = xia_china
			clr_title_flag = qing_china
			clr_title_flag = dai_china
			clr_title_flag = cheng_china
			clr_title_flag = liang_china
			clr_title_flag = song_china
			clr_title_flag = ming_china
			clr_title_flag = shu_china
			clr_title_flag = wu_china
			clr_title_flag = chu_china
			clr_title_flag = yue_china
			clr_title_flag = yin_china
			clr_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		#log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		#log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		#log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.18 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.18
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_18
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_18
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_18 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				NOT = {

					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}

			character_event = { id = grace.999 } # Chinese princess (and Grace) update
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.20 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				dynasty = 1051150 # Li
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = tang_china
				}
			}

narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.20
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_20
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_20
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_20 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

			clr_title_flag = qing_china
			clr_title_flag = dai_china
			clr_title_flag = cheng_china
			clr_title_flag = liang_china
			clr_title_flag = song_china
			clr_title_flag = ming_china
			clr_title_flag = shu_china
			clr_title_flag = wu_china
			clr_title_flag = chu_china
			clr_title_flag = yue_china
			clr_title_flag = yin_china
			clr_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		e_china = {
			set_name = "Shun Empire"
			adjective = "Shun"
			set_title_flag = shun_china
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.22 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					year = 1200
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = shun_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
		}
		name = EVTOPTE_NAMEOFCHINA_21 # More options!
		clr_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
		repeat_event = { id = nameofchina.21 }
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world

	id = nameofchina.22

##### Religion conversion

### The EoC converts religion, no longer Chinese Imperial

# Inform the EoC that all Grace will be lost, give the player the option to convert back
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.23
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_23
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_23
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = taoist_convert
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = e_china
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_dlc = "Jade Dragon"
				has_dlc = "Rajas of India"
			}
			OR = {
				secret_religion = taoist
				AND = {
					ai = no
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture_group = chinese_group
						culture = khitan
						culture = tangut
						culture = jurchen
						culture = mongol
						culture = viet
						culture_group = koreanic
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
						religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
						religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
						religion = bon # Tibet
						religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = chinese_pagan
						religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
						#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
						religion = korean_pagan
						religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
						religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
						religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					}
					NOT = {
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_23 # Convert to Taoist
		
		set_character_flag = taoist_convert
		
		religion = taoist
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOR = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = chinese_pagan
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					secret_religion = taoist
				}
				NOR = {
					religion_group = indian_group # Eastern
					religion = tengri_pagan # Likely for nomads, but not guaranteed...
					religion = zun_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it
					religion = bon # Tibet
					religion = ainu_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = chinese_pagan
					religion = chinese_pagan_reformed # Might be allowed to keep their religion if we change the conditions for Grace being enabled...
					#religion = shinto # If we want Shinto rulers to do this, we should check that they're not the EoJ or his liege
					religion = korean_pagan
					religion = korean_pagan_reformed # Disallow?
					religion = ryukyuan_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = sanamahi_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = dayak_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = melanesian_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					religion = viet_pagan # Somewhat close to China, so let them do it; if reformed, they shouldn't want to!
					culture_group = chinese_group
					culture = khitan
					culture = tangut
					culture = jurchen
					culture = mongol
					culture = viet
					culture_group = koreanic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_23 # Do not convert
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				secret_religion = taoist
			}
		}
		
		#log = "The Emperor of China is no longer using Grace!"
		# We are forced to use any_character here to account for deposed rulers, even though the scope is performance-intensive
		# This event should hopefully only fire rarely, though, so it should be fine
		
		# Clear out Imperial Princesses
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_unmarried
			remove_trait = dragon_bride_married
		}
		#log = "Chinsee princesses have lost their traits!"
				
		# Clear all Grace and stop tracking Grace characters
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = grace_character
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = grace
				value = 0
			}
			clr_character_flag = grace_character
		}
		
		#log = "All Grace has been removed from all characters!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = china_send_relief
			}
			remove_character_modifier = china_send_relief
		}
		
		#log = "All relief expeditions have been ended!"
		
		## Terminate all "Supply Horses" agreements
		#any_character = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#	}
		#	remove_character_modifier = china_supply_horses
		#}
		#
		##log = "All agreements to supply horses have been ended!"
		
		# Revoke all Chinese Trade Contracts
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
			}
			remove_character_modifier = chinese_imperial_trade_contract
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Trade Contracts have been ended!"
		
		# Remove all Chinese Peace Deals
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
			}
			remove_character_modifier = peace_deal_with_china
		}
		
		#log = "All Chinese Peace Deals have been ended!"
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.24 }
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world that all Grace is lost if the EoC picks that option
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.24
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_24
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_24
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_24 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
					trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
				}
			}
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_1
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_2
			remove_trait = kow_tow_completed_tier_3
		}
	}
}

		e_china = {
			NOR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china

				has_title_flag = zhou_china

				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china
				has_title_flag = dai_china
				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china

				has_title_flag = shun_china

		}
	}

	}

		}

		e_china = {
			clr_title_flag = tang_china

			clr_title_flag = wei_china
			clr_title_flag = qi_china
			clr_title_flag = zhou_china
			clr_title_flag = han_china
			clr_title_flag = qin_china
			clr_title_flag = yan_china
			clr_title_flag = zhao_china

		}

			set_name = "Tang Empire"
			adjective = "Tang"

					}
				}

				text = CREATE_CI_BLOODLINE

			}
		}

					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT

						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.26 }
		}

			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}

		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.26 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = chu_china
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Inform the EoC
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.27
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_27
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_27
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = taoist_convert
			}
		}
		has_landed_title = e_china
		# China is already named
		e_china = {
			OR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china

				has_title_flag = wei_china

				has_title_flag = han_china

character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.29
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = no
		}
		FROM = {
			title = e_china

### Creation

# The holder gets to pick a name
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.30
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_30
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_30
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kow_tow_travels
			}
			character_event = { id = JD.32299 } # Interrupt kowtow
		}
	}
	
	# Please select new China name!
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_tang_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = TANG
		
		primary_title = {
			set_name = "Tang Empire"
			adjective = "Tang"
			set_title_flag = tang_china
			add_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = real_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_flag = pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CREATE_FAKE_CI_BLOODLINE
				create_pretender_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.31 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					culture = karluk
					culture = turkish
				}
			}

				factor = 1000
				dynasty = 1051150 # Li
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_flag = tang_china
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_1
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_2
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_3
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_4
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_5
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_6
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_7
					has_character_flag = china_name_repeat_8
				}
			}
			china_or_pretender_can_be_jin_trigger = yes
		}
		
		name = JIN
		
		primary_title = {
			set_name = "Jin Empire"
			adjective = "Jin"
			set_title_flag = jin_china
			add_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}

### Destroy any empire if the EoC inherits it (or any non-e_china title if its holder becomes the EoC)

# Destroy the title
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.32
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_32
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_32
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			tier = emperor
			is_china_or_pretender_empire_trigger = yes
		}
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_32 # The Middle Kingdom is enough!
		
		# Keep China if you have it
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = e_china
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					NOT = {
						title = e_china
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				clr_title_flag = tang_china
				clr_title_flag = jin_china
				clr_title_flag = wei_china
				clr_title_flag = qi_china
				clr_title_flag = zhou_china
				clr_title_flag = han_china
				clr_title_flag = qin_china
				clr_title_flag = yan_china
				clr_title_flag = zhao_china
				clr_title_flag = liao_china
				clr_title_flag = yuan_china
				clr_title_flag = xia_china
				clr_title_flag = qing_china
				clr_title_flag = dai_china
				clr_title_flag = cheng_china
				clr_title_flag = liang_china
				clr_title_flag = song_china
				clr_title_flag = ming_china
				clr_title_flag = shu_china
				clr_title_flag = wu_china
				clr_title_flag = chu_china
				clr_title_flag = yue_china
				clr_title_flag = yin_china
				clr_title_flag = shun_china
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
		# Or keep a title matching your bloodline
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = emperor
					title_matches_my_chinese_bloodline_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			# First destroy unmatching titles
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					title_matches_my_chinese_bloodline_trigger = no
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				clr_title_flag = tang_china
				clr_title_flag = jin_china
				clr_title_flag = wei_china
				clr_title_flag = qi_china
				clr_title_flag = zhou_china
				clr_title_flag = han_china
				clr_title_flag = qin_china
				clr_title_flag = yan_china
				clr_title_flag = zhao_china
				clr_title_flag = liao_china
				clr_title_flag = yuan_china
				clr_title_flag = xia_china
				clr_title_flag = qing_china
				clr_title_flag = dai_china
				clr_title_flag = cheng_china
				clr_title_flag = liang_china
				clr_title_flag = song_china
				clr_title_flag = ming_china
				clr_title_flag = shu_china
				clr_title_flag = wu_china
				clr_title_flag = chu_china
				clr_title_flag = yue_china
				clr_title_flag = yin_china
				clr_title_flag = shun_china
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
			# Then destroy non-primary empires, if we somehow ended up with two pretender empires
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							NOT = {
								title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				clr_title_flag = tang_china
				clr_title_flag = jin_china
				clr_title_flag = wei_china
				clr_title_flag = qi_china
				clr_title_flag = zhou_china
				clr_title_flag = han_china
				clr_title_flag = qin_china
				clr_title_flag = yan_china
				clr_title_flag = zhao_china
				clr_title_flag = liao_china
				clr_title_flag = yuan_china
				clr_title_flag = xia_china
				clr_title_flag = qing_china
				clr_title_flag = dai_china
				clr_title_flag = cheng_china
				clr_title_flag = liang_china
				clr_title_flag = song_china
				clr_title_flag = ming_china
				clr_title_flag = shu_china
				clr_title_flag = wu_china
				clr_title_flag = chu_china
				clr_title_flag = yue_china
				clr_title_flag = yin_china
				clr_title_flag = shun_china
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
		# Or just keep your primary title
		else = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = emperor
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							NOT = {
								title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
				set_name = ""
				adjective = ""
				clr_title_flag = tang_china
				clr_title_flag = jin_china
				clr_title_flag = wei_china
				clr_title_flag = qi_china
				clr_title_flag = zhou_china
				clr_title_flag = han_china
				clr_title_flag = qin_china
				clr_title_flag = yan_china
				clr_title_flag = zhao_china
				clr_title_flag = liao_china
				clr_title_flag = yuan_china
				clr_title_flag = xia_china
				clr_title_flag = qing_china
				clr_title_flag = dai_china
				clr_title_flag = cheng_china
				clr_title_flag = liang_china
				clr_title_flag = song_china
				clr_title_flag = ming_china
				clr_title_flag = shu_china
				clr_title_flag = wu_china
				clr_title_flag = chu_china
				clr_title_flag = yue_china
				clr_title_flag = yin_china
				clr_title_flag = shun_china
				clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
				unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_33 # Keep being a pretender empire!
		
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		
		FROM = {
			make_primary_title = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				NOT = {
					title = FROM
				}
			}
			unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = nameofchina.35 } # Rename the empire
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					dynasty = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_33 # Stop being a pretender empire!
		
		FROM = {
			set_name = ""
			adjective = ""
			remove_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
			clr_title_flag = tang_china
			clr_title_flag = jin_china
			clr_title_flag = wei_china
			clr_title_flag = qi_china
			clr_title_flag = zhou_china
			clr_title_flag = han_china
			clr_title_flag = qin_china
			clr_title_flag = yan_china
			clr_title_flag = zhao_china
			clr_title_flag = liao_china
			clr_title_flag = yuan_china
			clr_title_flag = xia_china
			clr_title_flag = qing_china
			clr_title_flag = dai_china
			clr_title_flag = cheng_china
			clr_title_flag = liang_china
			clr_title_flag = song_china
			clr_title_flag = ming_china
			clr_title_flag = shu_china
			clr_title_flag = wu_china
			clr_title_flag = chu_china
			clr_title_flag = yue_china
			clr_title_flag = yin_china
			clr_title_flag = shun_china
			clr_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			set_government_type = muslim_government
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = tibetan_group
				OR = {
					religion = bon
					religion = buddhist
				}
				higher_tier_than = BARON
			}
			set_government_type = theocratic_feudal_government
		}
		else = {
			set_government_type = feudal_government
		}
		
		any_player = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					any_realm_province = {
						trade_route = silk_road
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			narrative_event = { id = nameofchina.34 }
		}
		
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				dynasty = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world if the pretender empire stops being a pretender empire
narrative_event = {
	id = nameofchina.34
	title = EVTTITLE_NAMEOFCHINA_34
	desc = EVTDESC_NAMEOFCHINA_34
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = no
		}
		name = EVTOPTA_NAMEOFCHINA_34 # I see... # TODO: Split based on claims, dynasty, etc.?
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		}
		name = EVTOPTB_NAMEOFCHINA_34 # As it should be!
	}
}

### Temple names

# on_death event to set temple names
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.36
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Historical EoCs (that held e_china) get their historical temple name
		# Tang
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_daizong
			}
			set_name = Daizong
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_dezong
			}
			set_name = Dezong
			set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = temple_name_shunzong

##### Various pings to fix scopes

# Inheritance within same dynasty - suddenly Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.37
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		ROOT = {
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = no
		}
		# China isn't already named
		e_china = {
			NOR = {
				has_title_flag = tang_china
				has_title_flag = jin_china
				has_title_flag = wei_china
				has_title_flag = qi_china
				has_title_flag = zhou_china
				has_title_flag = han_china
				has_title_flag = qin_china
				has_title_flag = yan_china
				has_title_flag = zhao_china
				has_title_flag = liao_china
				has_title_flag = yuan_china
				has_title_flag = xia_china
				has_title_flag = qing_china
				has_title_flag = dai_china
				has_title_flag = cheng_china
				has_title_flag = liang_china
				has_title_flag = song_china
				has_title_flag = ming_china
				has_title_flag = shu_china
				has_title_flag = wu_china
				has_title_flag = chu_china
				has_title_flag = yue_china
				has_title_flag = yin_china
				has_title_flag = shun_china
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.3 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

# Inheritance by other dynasty
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.38
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
		FROMFROM = {
			NOT = {
				dynasty = ROOT
			}
			has_acceptable_chinese_religion_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = nameofchina.5 days = 1 } # Fire the actual event
	}
}

# on_startup event to set the relevant flag(s)
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.42
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
	} 
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = e_china
			}
			update_global_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
			}
			add_global_pretender_china_name_flag_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# on_death event ensuring that dead Song emperors have their zhangokfutou
character_event = {
	id = nameofchina.43
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		government = chinese_imperial_government
		OR = {
			dynasty = 1051151 ### Song Dynasty, known in almost all official artwork as wearing their weird zhangokfutou
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_flag = song_china # If someone creates a "Song Empire", give them the proper headgear!
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_trait = dead_song_emperor
	}
}
